ciclo: 
    lw t0, 0(s0)
    add a0, a0, t0
    addi s0, s0, 4
    addi s1, s1, -1
    bne s1, zero, ciclo ^pIBjcbC0

control ^E9geqoC4

branch ^gVknSq9s

branch logic ^WaePWSTe

≈ ^e3iq7vR3

the instruction after the branch is always executed, just in case ∵ we have data hazard ^s6RgVgIj

branch prediction ^HC3flXvQ

follow behaviour of last branch ^CtNxUgyJ

if previously we branched, load instruction of branching ^BodyFuWy

if previously we not branched, load instruction of after branch ^XWXdhfaq

for i=1 to 5 ^wEFGeuGO

i=1 we load wrong instruction ^XjuSWNlh

i=2,3,4 we load right instruction ^ohueJZuO

i=5 we load wrong instruction ^QadI9hSL

old ^bbydCzEP

new ^ay3jm7Nr
